<Review>I visited this DMV for my wife's behind-the-wheel test. The only reason we drove down from San Jose to Watsonville is because we couldn't get an appointment in any of the DMVs of the Bay Area. The place is smaller than most of the DMVs of the Bay Area. For an 11:10 appointment, we were told that we can check in at 11, since we arrived early. There were only 2 DMV examiners on the test day which caused a long line of test applicants waiting in their cars to take their test. We waited for 25-30 mins for our chance to take the test. On reading some of the other reviews, I feel that's probably quite common. However, the examiner was really supportive and helpful. At the end of the test, he passed my wife and diligently pointed out the errors she made and provided recommendations for improvements. Upon entering the DMV to get her temporary license, we had to wait for another 15-20 minutes because no one was there at counter 9 and eventually the lady from counter 7 helped us.

Overall, this DMV appeared to be less crowded, there were enough parking spots available outside, though one should expect to wait out a while to take their behind-the-wheel test.<//Review>< rate>

< Date>

<rating>4< /rating>< review>
This is a great local pet store, a refreshing change 9003 Waterford Centre Blvd Suite #180, Austin, TX 78758 the big box pet stores. I asked if they were affiliated with the Big Al's pet store that used to be located near the Northwest corner of First Street and Los Angeles, and he said the he used to be the manager of that store. When it went it out of business, he decided to open a new pet store and asked the owner of the original Big Al's if he could use that name once it closed, which they agreed to. Big Al was the father of the owner. He has the same cat adoption volunteers come to the new Big Al's as used to visit the original. Prices are in line with the competition, but you get that small business service you miss from the big boys and girls. I recommend you visit Big Al's and give them your business, lest we be left with only chain stores to fill out needs. I don't want to be describing to my grandchildren what it was like to have a mom-and-pop store around.<//review>

< Text>
By far worst experience I have had at a McDonald's, If I could I would have given them half a star or no star. Traditionally I make breakfast from home but I went to this McDonald's because I wanted to try the new cinnamon roll.  When I arrived the drive-thru line was somewhat busy as it can always be because this is a popular location but I saw a sign that recommended going inside for takeout. I decided to go inside for takeout. I was the only person in line to order and there was a DoorDash person waiting as well. My order was fairly simple as I got one sausage egg McMuffin combo, an extra sausage McMuffin and both a blueberry muffin and a cinnamon roll. After about 10 minutes another DoorDash person came in and a few moments later that person's order was ready. This upset the original DoorDash person who mentioned that our orders have not been taken care of and we should have went our food first. This disgruntled door dash worker was able to get them to make his food next and then after a couple minutes they noticed I was still there so they made me what they thought was my order. When they made my order I noticed that they did not put everything in bag. I decided to open the bag in front of them to show them that the entire combo and orange juice were missing. The worker told me that I did not order a combo or orange juice so then I decided to pull up my receipt to check and was able to confirm that I ordered a combo and  an orange juice. she originally gave me the orange juice and apologize but then I mentioned what about my other breakfast sandwich and hash brown. She then told me again I did not order a combo and began to search for my order. During this whole time I noticed that my order was never put on a little screens that they use to make the orders in the back but rather they printed the receipt and just put it on the counter. Eventually after finding my receipt she then grabbed a hash brown and another sandwich.

All in all this location is not organized. They prioritize the drive-thru and DoorDash orders. The drive-thru is always busy so they want you to come in to make a delivery/takeout order but you have to watch them to make sure that you get what you pay for and that they make it correctly.

On a separate note I I must have been there over 20 minutes for this order and witnessed some type of  shift change over which is partially why try to express patience with them but the team members that were leaving seem more concerned about making their own orders to go home than helping any customers and both team members that came into did not wear a mask upon entering but rather waited until someone said something to then put on their mask. In my opinion this is very rude of a staff that expects this of their customers.</Text>
